The American health care debate isn‚Äôt really about value or efficiency ‚Äî the data is clear and convincing that under universal health care the population gets more care for a cheaper cost ‚Äî it's about philosophy.
I hear variations of this a lot. It‚Äôs true that universal health care systems ration health care (eg, wait times for elective surgeries). But the American system does this too, by pricing out certain people from receiving health care. https://t.co/6t5mY4uAfc
Study is here for those who want to check it out: https://t.co/9U1iP66ZAB
So in conclusion, a LIBERTARIAN THINK TANK just found that Medicare for all:		- Saves money compared to status quo	- Provides far more health care, in particular to the poor	- Could be done without bludgeoning workers with new taxes.
Very tl;dr, when businesses don‚Äôt have to pay their employees‚Äô health costs they‚Äôre lifted of a huge expense, which leads to a big rise in wages, which leads to more taxible income. https://t.co/IvgHpsUUPA
Ok but of course publicly funded health care is ultimately paid for by taxes so isn‚Äôt that a huge expense Not really, says Mercatus  ‚Äî again, a libertarian think tank! ‚Äî because it‚Äôs offset by removing the massive health costs people pay now.
Where does this money come from? Not from raising taxes, per the study, but from lowering prices paid to health care providers (insurance companies, hospitals, drug manufacturers, etc.) https://t.co/3ZaNs1fGAL
Who does this help the most? People who currently cannot afford health insurance. https://t.co/m6YAYWelC8
Mercatus found that Medicare for all would lead to massive savings which are mostly offset by increased utilization. Translation: people get a lot more health care for the same bill.
$32.6 trillion over a decade sounds like a lot, and is. But it‚Äôs actually a few hundred billion less than current projected health care costs.		Mercatus found the two plans cost about the same (just paid for differently, obviously) but what we get is very different under M4A
Let‚Äôs talk for a minute about this study from libertarian think tank Mercatus Center.
